A: Yes, RiskMAPs are Risk Evaluation and Mitigation Strategies. They're FDA-required programs for certain medications that have serious safety concerns but still provide benefits that outweigh the risks. For opioids, RiskMAPs typically include things like prescriber education, patient counseling requirements, and monitoring programs. The FDA can require these when they approve a drug or add them later if safety issues emerge.
